<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item&nbsp;2.02. Results of Operations and
Financial Condition</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On January&nbsp;10, 2005, Kraft Foods Inc.
issued a press release announcing that it realigned the financial reporting
structure for its North American businesses. The press release also announced
that Kraft will report the sugar confectionery brands it recently agreed to
sell as a &#147;discontinued business.&#148; A copy of the release and exhibits thereto
are attached as Exhibit 99.1.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item&nbsp;9.01. Financial Statements and
Exhibits</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">99.1 Release
dated January&nbsp;10, 2005 (furnished pursuant to Item 2.02).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
information in this Current Report is being furnished and shall not be deemed &#147;filed&#148;
for the purposes of Section&nbsp;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as
amended, or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that Section. The
information in this Current Report shall not be incorporated by reference into
any registration statement or other document pursuant to the Securities Act of
1933, as amended, expect as expressly set forth by specific reference therein.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2</font></p>

<body lang="EN-US" link="blue" vlink="purple">

<div>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit 99.1</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Kraft Realigns Financial Segment Structure for North America</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Company to Host Webcast on 2004 Full-Year and Fourth-Quarter Results</font></b></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">NORTHFIELD,
IL, January 10, 2005 &#151; Kraft Foods Inc. (NYSE:KFT), a global leader in branded
food and beverages, today announced that it realigned the financial reporting
structure for its North American businesses, following its agreement to sell
its sugar confectionery brands.&#160; These
changes will be reflected in the company&#146;s financial results, including in its
fourth-quarter and full-year 2004 results.</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The new
segment reporting structure separates the former U.S. Beverages &amp; Grocery
segment into a U.S. Beverages segment and a U.S. Grocery segment to provide
more focus on each business.&#160;
Additionally, the cereals business has been moved from the former U.S.
Beverages &amp; Grocery segment to the new U.S. Snacks &amp; Cereals segment to
benefit more fully from synergies among grain-based products like cereals,
cookies and crackers.</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
sugar confectionery brands Kraft recently agreed to sell will be reported as a
&#147;discontinued business,&#148; which excludes the results of this business from its
volume, revenue and operating companies income (OCI) measures, while
maintaining its impact on earnings per share until the sale is completed.&#160; These brands previously had been part of the
U.S. Snacks segment; the U.S. Cheese, Canada &amp; North America Foodservice
segment; and the company&#146;s two international segments.</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Attachments</font></u><font face="Times New Roman"> to this
release provide restated volume, net revenues and OCI for 2002, 2003 and the
first three quarters of 2004, reflecting the new segment structure and the
change in sugar confectionery.</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Under
the new structure, there are five North American reportable segments:</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">U.S.
Beverages, including coffee and refreshment beverages</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">U.S. Cheese,
Canada &amp; North America Foodservice</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">U.S.
Convenient Meals, including pizza, meats and meals</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">U.S.
Grocery, including desserts and enhancers</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">U.S. Snacks
&amp; Cereals, including biscuits, salted snacks and cereals</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kraft
will continue to report its International results within the same two
geographic segments: Europe, Middle East &amp; Africa; and Latin America
&amp;&nbsp;Asia Pacific.</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kraft plans to announce its 2004
fourth-quarter and full-year results, as well as an outlook for 2005, at approximately
4:05 p.m. ET on January 25, 2005.&#160; At 5
p.m. ET that day, the company will host a live audio webcast at kraft.com* to
discuss these results.&#160; An archived
rebroadcast will be available on kraft.com* for one year following the webcast.</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kraft Foods markets many of the world&#146;s
leading food brands, including <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Kraft</font></i> cheese, <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Maxwell</font></i>  <i><font style="font-style:italic;">House</font></i> and <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Jacobs</font></i> coffees, <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Nabisco</font></i> cookies
and crackers, <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Philadelphia</font></i> cream cheese, <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Oscar Mayer</font></i> meats, <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Post</font></i> cereals
and <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Milka</font></i> chocolates, in more than 150
countries.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">#&#160; #&#160; #</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">KRAFT FOODS INC.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">and Subsidiaries</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Discontinued Operations &amp;
Segment Realignment - Volume</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Quarterly
2002</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(lbs in millions)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">As a result of organizational changes, the company&#146;s
fourth quarter and full-year 2004 results will be presented in a new segment
structure.&#160; Additionally, the sugar
confectionery brands Kraft agreed to sell will be reported as a &#147;discontinued
business&#148;, which excludes the results of this business from its volume, net
revenues and operating companies income (OCI) measures, while maintaining its
impact on earnings per share until the sale is completed.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">KRAFT FOODS INC.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">and Subsidiaries</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Discontinued Operations &amp;
Segment Realignment - Net Revenues</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Quarterly
2002</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">($ in millions)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">As a result of organizational changes, the company&#146;s
fourth quarter and full-year 2004 results will be presented in a new segment
structure.&#160; Additionally, the sugar
confectionery brands Kraft agreed to sell will be reported as a &#147;discontinued
business&#148;, which excludes the results of this business from its volume, net
revenues and operating companies income (OCI) measures, while maintaining its
impact on earnings per share until the sale is completed.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">

<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">KRAFT FOODS INC.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">and Subsidiaries</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Discontinued Operations &amp;
Segment Realignment - Operating Companies Income</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Quarterly
2002</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">($ in millions)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">As a result of organizational changes, the company&#146;s
fourth quarter and full-year 2004 results will be presented in a new segment
structure.&#160; Additionally, the sugar
confectionery brands Kraft agreed to sell will be reported as a &#147;discontinued
business&#148;, which excludes the results of this business from its volume, net
revenues and operating companies income (OCI) measures, while maintaining its
impact on earnings per share until the sale is completed.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">KRAFT FOODS INC.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">and Subsidiaries</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Discontinued Operations &amp;
Segment Realignment - Volume</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Quarterly
2003</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(lbs in millions)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">As a result of organizational changes, the company&#146;s
fourth quarter and full-year 2004 results will be presented in a new segment
structure.&#160; Additionally, the sugar
confectionery brands Kraft agreed to sell will be reported as a &#147;discontinued
business&#148;, which excludes the results of this business from its volume, net
revenues and operating companies income (OCI) measures, while maintaining its
impact on earnings per share until the sale is completed.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">KRAFT FOODS INC.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">and Subsidiaries</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Discontinued Operations &amp;
Segment Realignment - Net Revenues</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Quarterly
2003</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">($ in millions)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">As a result of organizational changes, the company&#146;s
fourth quarter and full-year 2004 results will be presented in a new segment
structure.&#160; Additionally, the sugar
confectionery brands Kraft agreed to sell will be reported as a &#147;discontinued
business&#148;, which excludes the results of this business from its volume, net
revenues and operating companies income (OCI) measures, while maintaining its
impact on earnings per share until the sale is completed.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">KRAFT FOODS INC.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">and Subsidiaries</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Discontinued Operations &amp;
Segment Realignment - Operating Companies Income</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Quarterly
2003</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">($ in millions)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">As a result of organizational changes, the company&#146;s
fourth quarter and full-year 2004 results will be presented in a new segment
structure.&#160; Additionally, the sugar
confectionery brands Kraft agreed to sell will be reported as a &#147;discontinued
business&#148;, which excludes the results of this business from its volume, net
revenues and operating companies income (OCI) measures, while maintaining its
impact on earnings per share until the sale is completed.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
  </td>

  <p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:8.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Q1</font></b></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
  </td>

  <p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:8.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Q2</font></b></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">

  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">

<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">KRAFT FOODS INC.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">and Subsidiaries</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Discontinued Operations &amp;
Segment Realignment - Volume</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Quarterly
2004</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(lbs in millions)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">As a result of organizational changes, the company&#146;s
fourth quarter and full-year 2004 results will be presented in a new segment
structure.&#160; Additionally, the sugar
confectionery brands Kraft agreed to sell will be reported as a &#147;discontinued
business&#148;, which excludes the results of this business from its volume, net
revenues and operating companies income (OCI) measures, while maintaining its
impact on earnings per share until the sale is completed.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">KRAFT FOODS INC.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">and Subsidiaries</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Discontinued Operations &amp;
Segment Realignment - Net Revenues</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Quarterly
2004</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">($ in millions)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">As a result of organizational changes, the company&#146;s
fourth quarter and full-year 2004 results will be presented in a new segment
structure.&#160; Additionally, the sugar
confectionery brands Kraft agreed to sell will be reported as a &#147;discontinued
business&#148;, which excludes the results of this business from its volume, net revenues
and operating companies income (OCI) measures, while maintaining its impact on
earnings per share until the sale is completed.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">KRAFT FOODS INC.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">and Subsidiaries</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Discontinued Operations &amp;
Segment Realignment - Operating Companies Income</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Quarterly
2004</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">($ in millions)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">As a result of organizational changes, the company&#146;s
fourth quarter and full-year 2004 results will be presented in a new segment
structure.&#160; Additionally, the sugar
confectionery brands Kraft agreed to sell will be reported as a &#147;discontinued
business&#148;, which excludes the results of this business from its volume, net
revenues and operating companies income (OCI) measures, while maintaining its
impact on earnings per share until the sale is completed.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
